Negotiations on the Sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway

Soviet Russia Demands a High Price: The Railway is Priced at 210 Million Rubles 16

Japan Uses Non-Aggressive Mediation as a Threat

(Tokyo) The Soviet Russian Embassy issued a detailed statement tonight regarding the negotiations on the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway, stating that Soviet Russia is willing to sell all rights to the Chinese Eastern Railway for 210,000,000 gold rubles. (4th Reuters Dispatch)

(Tokyo) The Russo-Manchu conference held yesterday lasted more than five hours. According to a statement released today, the Russian and Manchu representatives presented proposals and their own views on the Chinese Eastern Railway and will discuss them at the plenary meeting on Wednesday. It is heard that the conditions put forward by both sides are far apart, but not irreconcilable. Soviet Russia is now asking for 210,000,000 gold rubles for the railway itself, plus 40,000,000 gold rubles for the transfer of rights to the North Manchurian Soviet Russian timber yards and other facilities related to the railway. "Manchukuo" is giving 50 million Japanese yen, excluding the assets belonging to the railway. (4th Reuters Dispatch)

(Tokyo) The proposals made by the Russian representatives at the third meeting on the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway differed greatly from those of "Manchukuo", namely that the price demanded by the Russian side for the Chinese Eastern Railway and all its ancillary businesses was ten times more than the amount expected by "Manchukuo". Therefore, on the 4th, the two sides studied whether their respective demands were justified in preparation for renegotiation at the next meeting. (4th Joint Dispatch)

(Tokyo) The third meeting on the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway opened at 3:30 PM on the 3rd. Lieutenant Colonel Suzuki of Japan and the Director of the First Division of Western Europe and America were present. Today, the Russian Ambassador, Yurenev, chaired the meeting. The Soviet Russian representatives first stated the principled direction of the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway, followed by the "Manchukuo" representatives, who also expounded the fundamental principles of purchasing the railway. Afterwards, the two sides discussed various issues until 9:00 PM, when the meeting adjourned. At the same time, the following press release was issued: "At today's meeting, both the Russian and Manchu sides presented proposals and views on the Chinese Eastern Railway issue. These proposals will be reviewed at the next meeting. The next meeting is scheduled to open at 2:30 PM on the afternoon of the 5th." The meeting also decided to issue a press release after each meeting. (4th Japan Union Electric Dispatch)

(Tokyo) On the third day of the meeting on the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway, the Russian and Manchu sides presented specific matters and announced the railway prices. Therefore, the meeting was quite tense. Russian Chairman Representative Ambassador Yurenev and other representatives repeatedly spoke to explain the reasonable basis for the Russian proposal. The Manchukuo representatives, Ding Shiyuan and Vice Minister Ōhashi, also explained the Manchurian point of view. The Russian proposal yesterday contained many political elements, and there was a huge disparity in the price of the Eastern Railway claimed by both sides. There are still many twists and turns ahead. (4th Japan Union Electric Dispatch)

(Tokyo) In the negotiations on the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway, the results of the third meeting yesterday showed that there was a large disparity between the opinions of Russia and Manchu. It is expected that there will inevitably be disputes in the future, namely (1) Regarding the counterpart objects of the transfer, the Manchurian side wanted to include the Soviet Russian co-management rights of the Chinese Eastern Railway and the ancillary businesses of the Chinese Eastern Railway, while the Soviet Russian side insisted on the ownership of the Chinese Eastern Railway and proposed to value the ancillary businesses separately. (2) Regarding the basis for valuation, the Manchurian side wanted to base it on the economic value after the independence of "Manchukuo", while the Soviet Russian side wanted to base it on the investment conditions during the imperial era and the purport of the 1924-1925 memorandum, namely that the Soviet Russian side wanted to actively acknowledge the value for future valuation, while the Manchurian side was passive. (3) Although the selling price has not been specifically determined, there is already a huge gap between the claims of both sides. The Soviet Russian side is asking for a very high price. If they do not humbly and calmly deal with the situation and engage in compromises, there will be many twists and turns ahead. (4th Electric Communication Dispatch)

(Tokyo) It is heard that the content of the Russian representative's proposal at yesterday's meeting is as follows: (1) The Russian side will sell the western section of the Chinese Eastern Railway from Manchuria Station to Harbin, the eastern section from Harbin to Suifenhe, and the southern section from Harbin to Kuanchengzi (the Russian side stated the price, but it cannot be made public now). (2) The ancillary businesses of the Chinese Eastern Railway, such as coal mines, forests, power plants, and other various affiliated businesses, will also be sold together with the railway. (3) The so-called French debt and the protests of the Chinese government regarding the Chinese Eastern Railway are not an issue. (4th Joint Dispatch)

(Nanjing) In yesterday's negotiations on the Chinese Eastern Railway, there was no specific deliberation on any item because the claims of the two countries were quite far apart, and in terms of the amount of money, the values stated by both sides were also more than one billion apart. Therefore, there were difficulties early on. If the Russian side does not have a compromise attitude in the future and the negotiations break down, the foreign affairs authorities said that the Japanese side is not actively mediating. (4th Electric Communication Dispatch)

(Tokyo) According to a publicity by the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Russian side raised the issue of the puppet Manchu severing the Suifenhe transfer point at yesterday's Chinese Eastern Railway negotiations and said that "Manchukuo" should be responsible for compensating its losses. Puppet Manchu is very dissatisfied with this point and plans to cite six reasons to refute the Russian claim at tomorrow's meeting. (4th China United Electric Dispatch)

Stumbled on Golden Reefs, the World Economic Conference is Shelved

The General Assembly Will be Convened Tomorrow to Decide on a Way to Postpone the Meeting 17

European Countries Issue a Joint Declaration on Gold

Explaining the Need to Maintain Currency Prices

Almost Officially Declaring a Currency War on the United States

(London) The core leadership committee of the Economic Conference met this morning and decided that the core leadership should convene a plenary meeting on Thursday to announce a recess. It was also decided that the various working committees that can work should proceed as usual until Thursday. The proposal for a recess was put forward by the Dutch Ambassador, Kurrien, and seconded by the British representative, Simon, and the French representative, Bonnet. The US representative, Cox, did not vote in favor. It is heard that the US will oppose the recess. British Prime Minister MacDonald and Commercial Secretary Runciman neither approved nor opposed the proposal, but said that experts still have time to discuss the conference issues on the new basis of the US President's declaration. The core leadership plenary meeting is scheduled to be held at 4:00 PM this afternoon. The postponement proposal now seems certain to be passed. If so, the core leadership will still exist to maintain the conference mechanism. (4th Reuters News Agency Dispatch)

(London) The World Economic Conference has run aground on the reefs of gold. The stalemate caused by President Roosevelt's declaration cannot be broken. What remains to be decided is the conditions for the postponement. Today's afternoon meeting has almost three ways: (1) Complete abandonment of the conference; (2) Preservation of the conference's operating mechanism; (3) Postponement of the meeting after granting the chairman the power to reconvene the meeting when stability is obtained in the future. It is said that the third method is the best. Since the recess is directly due to the issue of stabilizing currency prices, it is expected that the official date for reopening the meeting cannot be predetermined. (4th Reuters News Agency Dispatch)

(London) The five European countries that maintain the gold standard, France, Italy, Belgium, the Netherlands, and Switzerland, issued a joint declaration, saying:

"The governments signing this declaration are convinced that maintaining their currency prices is a fundamental plan for the world economic recovery and for restoring credit activities, and it is a guarantee of the social progress created by the countries. Therefore, they reaffirm their firm will to maintain a freely operating gold standard within the current monetary law structure at the current gold parity in each country, and request each central bank to maintain close cooperation to give this declaration the greatest effectiveness."

This declaration was signed at a meeting at the Savoy Hotel, where the French representative was staying, in response to the US President's statement on US monetary policy.

The British delegation is expected to issue a separate declaration, but it has not yet been issued. It is heard that at least for the moment, the British territories will not issue an official declaration. (3rd National Electric Dispatch)

(London) Since the United States opposed the temporary stabilization plan, the French representatives refused to attend the afternoon meeting of the core group committee and consulted with the representatives of the Netherlands, Belgium, Switzerland, Poland, and Italy to draft a declaration reaffirming the maintenance of the gold standard.

It is said that the central banks will be instructed to cooperate to maintain the current parity of their respective currencies with gold. This declaration is tantamount to declaring a currency war on the United States. The meeting is expected to break down as a result, so most representatives now advocate an immediate recess. (3rd National Electric Dispatch)

American Representatives Oppose Prolonging the Conference to Avoid Responsibility for Failure 18

Will Shift the Focus of the Conference

Proposal to Raise World Prices

(London) At a meeting this morning of the American delegation, Secretary of State Hull stated that the work of the Economic Conference must proceed and that subsequent work must focus on raising world prices. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

(London) Members of the American delegation regard President Roosevelt's declaration as a great misfortune. Although the American delegation will oppose extending the conference, if an extension is passed, the American delegation will support the second or third options. It is reported that the American representatives are currently divided on these two options. It is understood that several American representatives feel that their current position is extremely complex and that no progress can be made, because the American president's remarks have caused intense anti-American sentiment, making it impossible to achieve anything. (Reuters dispatch, 4th) (London) The American delegation is dissatisfied with the idea that the responsibility for extending the Economic Conference lies with President Roosevelt and is planning to take surprising action at the main steering committee meeting this afternoon. It is expected that the American delegation will present a concrete plan to the conference to show that the United States is willing to cooperate. Some say that the American proposal will be related to raising world prices. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

Roosevelt's Cabinet Holds Meeting on Cruiser 19

(New York) Today's newspapers report that there is disagreement between the American president and the American representatives regarding the atmosphere of the World Economic Conference. A dispatch from Annapolis to the New York Tribune states that Roosevelt's cabinet held a meeting today on the cruiser Indianapolis, deciding that the Economic Conference should continue, and should not be terminated due to the gold bloc's dissatisfaction with American policy. However, a dispatch from London to the same newspaper states that the American delegation now holds the view that continuing the meeting is essentially useless, and that even if an effort is made to reduce tariffs, no assistance will be obtained. The newspaper also states that the American cabinet is eager to avoid responsibility for disrupting the conference. The New York Times reports that if blame is attributed to the American attitude, President Roosevelt is willing to take responsibility for the conference's failure, but official opinion is that foreign countries cannot gracefully withdraw from the conference. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

France Firmly Insists on Maintaining the Gold Standard 20

Jointly with Gold Bloc Countries to Maintain the Gold Standard

Will Build High Tariff Barriers to Prevent the Entry of American Goods

(Paris) Before departing for England, French Finance Minister Bonnet made a statement to reporters, reiterating that the French government has no intention of abandoning the gold standard, as France's view has not changed. Bonnet stated, "The various facts we see at present not only do not weaken France's view, but can further strengthen it, as it is in accordance with the facts." Regarding domestic issues, Bonnet stated that the treasury's situation is extremely satisfactory and that it is appropriate to issue another batch of public bonds at this time to prepare for the future. (Havas dispatch, 3rd)

(Paris) The attitude of the French delegation to the London Economic Conference has now been clearly expressed without any doubt. French Finance Minister Bonnet had lunch with Prime Minister Daladier on Sunday, and the two had a long conversation. Afterwards, he consulted with Moret, the governor of the Bank of France. On the same afternoon, French President Lebrun delivered an important speech in Besancon, stating, "If currency continues to fluctuate, then any effective treaties or permanent agreements that France might join in the future are merely empty talk." Bonnet returned to London on Sunday evening. According to official statements, the French representatives' attitude from now on is to unconditionally abide by the current strategy of the countries in the continental gold standard bloc in order to seek currency stability. (National Telegraph, 3rd) (Paris) Because the situation at the London Economic Conference is not very smooth, the French government feels that it is possible to raise tariff rates, so this morning it requested extraordinary powers from the parliament. Prime Minister Daladier also explained to the Socialist Party delegation afterwards that the extraordinary powers requested by the government do not tend towards absolute power, and will not diminish the sovereignty of the parliament. (Havas dispatch, 4th)

(Paris) The French government has begun preparations to prevent American goods from entering the French market. According to reliable sources, the French cabinet has tentatively decided that the current tariff truce will not be continued after it expires on July 31, and that import duties on American goods will be increased to protect the domestic market. (National Telegraph, 3rd)

Conference Affairs Suddenly Stagnate 21

(London) There is much speculation as to whether the various committees can continue to work beneficially in New Campton or elsewhere. The most promising committees, such as the currency group, the silver group, and the commercial group, have all stalled directly or indirectly due to the American attitude. The wheat group and the production and marketing group among the various committees may be expected to proceed as usual. Some say that these committees may establish temporary offices in Geneva, because participating countries already have agencies in Geneva, which can save the cost of establishing agencies in London. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

French Representatives Absent from Currency Technical Group Meeting, Meeting Fails to Achieve Quorum 22

(London) At the meeting of the technical subcommittee of the currency committee's ad hoc committee this afternoon, the French representatives did not attend, and the meeting was adjourned indefinitely. The absence of the French representatives has given rise to all sorts of unfounded rumors. Although America's refusal to participate in the currency stabilization plan has forced the work of the Economic Conference to be temporarily suspended, France does not disregard the work of the various committees because of this, and it does not take the future of the Economic Conference lightly. At this time, there are indeed those who advocate extending the Economic Conference, but France has never made such a proposal. (Havas dispatch, 3rd)

Opinions on Currency and Silver Subcommittees Still Differ 23

(London) The World Economic Conference's currency committee, the subcommittee dealing with the silver issue, met this morning, chaired by American representative Pittman. Opinions were exchanged on whether a compromise could be reached between silver-producing and silver-storing countries. It was decided to continue private talks, and to report to the subcommittee once a satisfactory result has been achieved. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

Representatives from Canada and Russia in Heated Debate at Economic Committee's Production and Sales Group 24

(London) The Economic Committee's subcommittee discussing the organization of production and sales issues discussed the timber issue today, deciding to organize a special subcommittee to conduct a review. During the meeting, the Canadian representative launched a fierce attack on the Soviet Union. In his view, the Soviet Union was disrupting the world timber market with unfair competition. The Soviet representative stood up to defend, saying that the Soviet Union's foreign trade monopoly policy could at least guarantee that Russia would abide by the various agreements signed in the future. (Havas dispatch, 3rd)

Britain Makes Last-Ditch Effort, Does Not Believe Conference Will Fail Abruptly 25

(London) Gold bloc countries are considering raising the issue of adjourning the World Economic Conference, but British Prime Minister MacDonald and his cabinet members held meetings with representatives of British dominions repeatedly in the morning and afternoon. The situation is tense, but the British Prime Minister still does not admit defeat. (Reuters dispatch, 3rd)

(London) It is reported that MacDonald is currently striving to maintain the survival of the conference, at least to reach a temporary agreement on economic issues before adjourning. However, European representatives believe that President Roosevelt's rejection is so firm that continuing the meeting is a waste of effort. These people also expressed deep shock at the American declaration. (National Telegraph, 3rd)

British Government Declares Its Attitude: Maintain Freedom to Equalize and Seek Self-Protection 26

(London) The British government today reiterated in the House of Commons that Britain's ultimate goal is to restore the gold standard when stable conditions can be guaranteed. Treasury representative Hall-Billyshaw declared that we must retain complete freedom to choose the timing of equalization. He has given due consideration to the point raised by the questioner that many British merchants believe that attempting to stabilize the exchange market without first ensuring a sufficient amount of trade is inconsistent with proper procedures and is detrimental to British commerce. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

American Declaration Modified Several Times, Wording Firm and Vehement 27

(London) The American declaration on monetary policy was changed again by a telegram from the American president before it was released, making it far more firm and vehement than the summary that Hull had previously distributed to the representatives for their review. Even the American delegation was as surprised by it as the European representatives. As a result, the situation at the meetings yesterday and today has been fluctuating, and the attitude of the leaders of the gold standard countries has also changed from soft to hard. (National Telegraph, 3rd)

Small Groups Meet Frequently, Currency is the Focus of Discussion 28

(London) After the American declaration was released yesterday, representatives from various countries held small group meetings to discuss currency issues. There was also such a meeting at the hotel where the Italian representatives were staying. Italian Finance Minister Jung spent time welcoming an Italian flying squadron in London. Upon hearing news of the economic conference crisis, he immediately flew back to join this small group meeting. (National Telegraph, 4th)

Economic Conference Leaves Only a Corpse, Vehement Words of a Certain Representative 29

(London) Now that Europe recognizes that stabilizing currency is necessary for economic and financial recovery, it is expected that a currency war will occur in the future. A certain well-known representative, anticipating this currency war, stated today that the Economic Conference has already died. The current question is only whether to apply embalming to this corpse, or to let it decay. (National Telegraph, 3rd)

American Policy Inconsistent, Pittman's Proposal Wavering 30

(London) The American delegation has decided to oppose the movement to adjourn the Economic Conference at the current stage. The American delegation cannot agree on whether to withdraw the Pittman proposal of June 19. Some believe that this proposal contradicts the American president's position as expressed in Hull's statement. The Pittman proposal advocates reducing the legal gold reserve to a uniform 25 percent and advocates restoring silver coinage. (Reuters dispatch, 3rd)

America Advocates Both Gold and Silver, Silver Supporters Delighted 31

(London) Supporters of silver are delighted to hear President Roosevelt's statement that either gold alone or both gold and silver can be used as currency reserves, pointing to this as a direct response to the purely gold standard proposals of France and others. Londoners are now talking entirely about the American president's remarks and are waiting for the actions of the gold bloc countries. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

British and American Exchange Market Situation 32

(London) With the stabilization of currency now hopeless, the main steering committee's convocation of the full conference to announce the decision to adjourn did not affect the foreign exchange market. The market situation today remains the same as yesterday. The US dollar is still under attack. The US dollar opened at 4.485 today, and soon fell to 4.53, a new low since Britain abandoned the gold standard. It later rose to 4.475 due to purchases from continental Europe. The market is filled with pessimism, and fluctuations are too drastic, making it very difficult to trade US dollars. (Reuters dispatch, 4th)

(New York) After President Roosevelt's declaration refusing to stabilize currency was released, Wall Street rallied, with a vehemence not seen since 1929. The US dollar exchange rate fell sharply, and the number of shares traded in various securities reached 7 million, mostly up by about one and a quarter points. (Havas dispatch, 3rd)

Expresses Adopting the Same Stance

Dollar's Decline Causes Some Panic

(Tokyo) According to news from Japanese financial circles, the meeting has reached a stalemate because the American president refused to address the issue of stabilizing exchange rates proposed by European gold standard countries. Japan is taking the same action as the United States, standing on the side of non-gold standard countries. (China United Press, 4th)

(Tokyo) The Economic Conference has been completely pessimistic due to the United States' declaration opposing exchange agreements, and the world's economic war is increasingly intensifying. It is impossible to predict how far the American expansion panic will cause the US dollar to fall, which is extremely worthy of attention. If the trend continues, the British-American exchange rate will inevitably reach 50 cents per US dollar, and the Japanese-American exchange rate will inevitably reach 28 cents per US dollar. Although the rising prices of American cotton, silk, wheat, etc., do not affect Japan above the exchange rate decline, it is worthy of attention whether it will continue in the future. (Dentsu, 4th)

Current Commentary

China's Technical Cooperation with the League of Nations 35

— Zi

A Havas dispatch from Geneva on the 3rd stated that Song Ziwen presented a technical cooperation plan to the League of Nations Administrative Council, requesting the appointment of a liaison officer, and stated that the League of Nations Administrative Council was prepared to organize a special committee to take beneficial measures. This event should attract more attention from the Chinese people than the cotton and wheat loan, and the cotton and wheat loan was a sudden piece of news, while China's technical cooperation with the League of Nations has a history of more than three years to trace. Now, let us first describe the history of this matter.

During the spring of the 20th year, the director of the League of Nations Labor Bureau, the Minister of Health, and the water conservancy commissioner came to China to investigate. Song Ziwen, in his capacity as Minister of Finance of the National Government, sent a letter of cooperation request to the League of Nations, and at the same time established the National Economic Committee to establish a foundation for cooperation. Soon after, Song's "Ten-Year Construction Plan" and the League of Nations Labor Bureau and the Administrative Council's "Ten-Year Plan for the Development of China" were published successively. The League of Nations' Ten-Year Plan for the Development of China was based on the Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan, and its main points were: (1) to open up 30,000 acres of Chinese wasteland, (2) to expand China's railways, highways, air routes, and other transportation businesses, (3) to build several seaports along the Chinese coast, (4) to build 8 million tons of merchant ships for sea and inland river commercial transportation, and (5) to build large factories to manufacture objects needed by the Chinese people. After this plan was made public, the Japanese immediately clamored that the League of Nations was preparing to co-manage China. Three months after the September 18th Incident, Japanese commentator Reietsu Ienaga pointed out in his essay that Song's cooperation with the League of Nations had aroused the opposition and conspired with Japan to resist the movement, causing the surprise attack in Shenyang. Although Ienaga's words are not entirely credible, there is a common understanding among informed people that these two events are not without any relationship. After the national crisis, the League of Nations educational experts came to China to investigate before the January 28th Shanghai War. Recently, League of Nations legal experts also came to Nanjing to reorganize our country's administrative laws and regulations. The matter of cooperation between China and the League of Nations did not stop due to the resistance to Japan, which is also obvious.

Now that the Tanggu Truce has been signed for more than a month, and the Dalian Conference is the day for important Sino-Japanese consultations, Song reported to the League of Nations Administrative Council the plan that "China has decided to step up construction work in several provinces and regions to make them model areas," requesting the designation of a technician to act as a closer liaison. We have not been able to read Song's documents on building several model provinces and regions in China, and we have not been able to obtain appropriate materials for discussion on this matter. However, there seems to be no item in the previous "Ten-Year Construction Plan" and "Ten-Year Plan for the Development of China" to establish model provinces and regions. Is this new plan being adjusted to reality due to the change in international forces in China, changing the construction of the entire China to the construction of several provinces with small scopes?

The use of foreign capital and foreign technology is neither purely beneficial nor purely harmful. It depends on the ability of the user. In the past, both the United States and Japan used foreign investment to build their countries, but the Congo and Egypt cannot be mentioned on the same day. The Soviet Union is now using American technicians and American machinery to carry out its five-year construction plan, and the construction results have shocked the world. Can China's technical cooperation with the League of Nations follow the Soviet Union and create amazing construction results? Or will it be controlled, as the Japanese cursed, leading to a co-management situation? This is why we cannot help but be fearful when we hear the sound of cooperation.

(Dentsu dispatch, 4th)

The Budgets of Jiangsu and Zhejiang Provinces are Severely Deficient 38

Gu Zhutong and Lu Diping Have Both Left Beijing

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan has not yet come up with a concrete solution for the budget proposals of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces in the 22nd year. Regarding the construction expenditure in Zhejiang province, the actual difference is more than 5 million, of which local construction expenditure accounts for about 2 million. The Zhejiang Provincial Government firmly requests the Central Government to restore the monthly subsidy of 150,000 yuan to complete local construction. More than 3 million are border road construction costs related to national defense that the Central Government has set a deadline for completion, and it is hoped that the Central Government will provide subsidies. The financial situation in Jiangsu is even more complicated, and the Central Government's current strength is really helpless. The authorities of the two provinces now hope that if the salt tax increase can achieve its goal, Zhejiang can increase its annual income by more than 1.4 million, and Jiangsu can also increase its revenue by more than 2.6 million. The Central Government did not immediately approve it. President Wang said that it could be discussed at length. On the 4th, Chairman Gu Zhutong of Jiangsu and Hall Chief Shu Shiyou returned to Zhenjiang, and Chairman Lu Diping of Zhejiang and Hall Chief Zhou Junyan returned to Hangzhou. The financial problems of the two provinces can only be fully resolved after Song Ziwen returns to the country. According to Zhou Junyan, Zhejiang's financial start-up methods are not without hope. For example, clearing the land throughout the province, reorganizing lost grain land, and reorganizing taxes to be paid can increase the field tax by 60% without increasing the burden on the people. However, the cost of clearing the land during the event is almost 20 to 30 million, and Zhejiang province does not have this financial capacity at this time. (Special dispatch, 4th)

The Panchen Lama's Return to Tibet 39

(Nanjing) Panchen's representatives, Anqin Wang Luojie, etc., telegraphed from Tibet to Beijing, saying that after arriving in Tibet to visit the Dalai Lama, the Dalai Lama's intentions were very good, and he repeatedly expressed his welcome for Panchen to return to Tibet. The time is up to him, but he has not mentioned the arrangements after returning to Tibet. According to those familiar with the situation in Tibet, Panchen intends to restore the management power of Tsang, while the Dalai Lama is still unwilling to give up the power of Tsang. Therefore, it is difficult to determine when Panchen's return to Tibet can be realized. (Special dispatch, 4th)

Ministries of Industry and Finance Confer on Coal Industry Bonds 40

A Decision Can Only Be Made After Song Returns to the Country

(Nanjing) Minister Chen Gongbo of the Ministry of Industry, Mining Division Chief Huang Jintao, and the Ministry of Finance discussed the 20 million coal industry bond case. The Ministry of Industry's opinion is that the issuance of this bond does not conflict with the existing bonds, and all repayment of principal and interest will be borne by the miners themselves, and it will be issued soon. However, the Ministry of Finance's opinion is that although this coal industry bond is borne by the miners themselves for the repayment of principal and interest, it is considered a formal national bond after passing through the Ministry, and the government has a corresponding responsibility. If merchants issue it themselves, it is called a corporate bond, and the government may not intervene. Therefore, the Ministry should carefully consider whether or not to issue coal bonds to avoid future worries. Even if miners guarantee the stability of the principal and interest, a decision will only be made after Minister Song returns to the country. (Special dispatch, 4th)

Soviet Russia Apologizes to Japan and Promises to Punish Those Responsible for the Death of Japanese Fishermen

Reuters, Moscow, 3rd – The Soviet Deputy Commissar for Foreign Affairs, Sokolnikov, told Japanese Ambassador Ota today that the incident of three Japanese fishermen being shot dead in Kamchatka has been investigated and confirmed to be true. He expressed apologies on behalf of the Soviet government and guaranteed that the Soviet government would punish the Soviet personnel involved in the incident.

TASS, Moscow, 3rd – The Acting Soviet Commissar for Foreign Affairs, Sakolnikov, reported to Japanese Ambassador Ota yesterday on the results of the investigation into the incident of Soviet guards shooting three Japanese fishermen on the coast of Kamchatka. The investigation was conducted by Soviet officials in Kamchatka under the supervision of representatives of the Foreign Affairs Committee. He informed Ota that although the investigation was not yet complete, certain facts had been fully confirmed. It was reported that a conflict occurred between Soviet coast guards and three Japanese fishermen on June 15 in the Olka Cape area on the east coast of Kamchatka (it was previously reported that the incident occurred at Kronotsky Cape, where there were no Soviet coast guards, which was incorrect). After the conflict, the coast guards at Olka Cape disappeared, and their whereabouts are still unknown but are being searched for. Documents found in the office of the coast guard station confirm that the incident of the three Japanese fishermen being shot dead was indeed true and that the fishermen were shot for not allowing the coast guards to use weapons. Sakolnikov also informed Ota that the Soviet government would severely punish those directly or indirectly responsible for the case and would also compensate the families of the murdered fishermen for the losses they suffered due to the improper actions of the coast guards.

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs plans to accept this note, and the Tomi Maru incident has been completely resolved.

Dentsu, Tokyo, 4th – At 10:00 AM today, a regular cabinet meeting was held at the Prime Minister's residence, attended by Army Minister Araki, Navy Minister Osumi, and other cabinet members. The Success of Soviet Diplomacy: Security Pacts Signed with Various Countries in Eastern Europe and the Near East; Similar Treaties to be Concluded with the Little Entente; "Aggressor" Defined in Treaties

Le Matin, London, 3rd – Today, Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov and representatives of Persia, Afghanistan, Turkey, Poland, Romania, Latvia, and Estonia signed an unprecedented security pact containing a definition of "aggressor." He then made a brief speech, stating that all countries would be invited to join the pact. Finland is about to join, and China is expected to join in the future. Today, Lithuania did not join the pact due to Poland's opposition to Lithuania signing because of the dispute over the Vilnius region. However, Litvinov has stated that the Soviet Union will conclude a treaty of the same nature with Lithuania separately.

Le Matin, Berlin, 4th – News from various parts of Europe indicates that the governments and newspapers of the countries that signed the multilateral non-aggression pact in London are extremely excited about the new treaty. Litvinov declared in London that the signatory countries have a total population of 265 million people and that peace is guaranteed by this new treaty. News from the Romanian capital states that Romania views this new treaty as a new guarantee of non-aggression against Bessarabia. Semi-official news from Prague states that Czechoslovakia and Yugoslavia will soon join the new treaty. News from the Polish capital states that the Polish Foreign Minister declared that the new treaty is of utmost importance and that Poland is particularly satisfied. Furthermore, according to a detailed analysis by the Polish Telegraph Agency, Poland is even more pleased that Turkey has signed the new treaty because it allows Poland to maintain its traditional friendship with Turkey.

Reuters, London, 3rd – Today, the Soviet Union, Afghanistan, Lithuania, Estonia, Persia, Poland, Romania, and Turkey signed an important non-aggression treaty here. The treaty is divided into five sections and one appendix, which defines an aggressor as follows:

(1) The first to declare war;

(2) Occupying the territory of another country without declaring war;

(3) Attacking the land, sea, or air forces of the other party with land, sea, or air forces;

(4) Blockading the coast and seaports of another country;

(5) Supporting, within its own territory, gangs that invade the territory of another country and refusing the request of the invaded country to take appropriate steps to stop such gangs within its territory.

The appendix declares that the signatory countries shall not use any event as a pretext for aggression.

Reuters, London, 3rd – At the signing of the non-aggression treaty today, Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov issued a statement saying that the definition of aggressor had been proposed in Geneva, but it was considered inconvenient for certain countries. Therefore, he now wishes to include this definition in a treaty only between a limited number of countries. This treaty is a new link in strengthening peaceful relations between the Soviet Union and its neighboring countries. The Soviet government is now prepared to sign similar treaties with countries around the world.

Havas, London, 3rd – It is reported that the Soviet Union will soon sign a treaty with the countries of the Little Entente (Romania has already signed this treaty with the Soviet Union) that defines an aggressor. It is also reported that similar negotiations will be conducted between the Soviet Union and Italy.

Reuters, London, 4th – The conclusion of the non-aggression pact between the Soviet Union and Afghanistan, Estonia, Latvia, Persia, Poland, Romania, and Turkey has been widely discussed in the lounges of the People's Economic Conference today, and has been described as Litvinov's strategy. Someone asked a Soviet official, "Why are China, Japan, and Manchukuo not included?" The official replied, "Oh, our work is not yet finished."

Higher Court's Response to the Chen Peng Appeal (Prosecutor Asks to Uphold the Original Sentence)

The case of Chen Duxiu, Peng Shuzhi, and other leaders of the Trotskyist faction of the Communist Party has been separately sentenced by the Suzhou Higher Court. Chen Duxiu, Peng Shuzhi, Pu Yifan, Guo Jinghao, Wang Wu, Wang Zhaoqun, Wang Ziping, and He Afang have been sentenced to imprisonment. Wang Jiantang and Liang Youguang were found innocent. They are being held at the Jiangning District Court Detention Center. Wang Jiantang and Liang Youguang have already been released. Wang Ziping and He Afang have waived their right to appeal. The Central Committee of the Kuomintang believed that Wang Ziping should be dealt with according to party discipline, and has transferred the matter to the Suzhou Higher Court. The Central Committee has prepared a document to the detention center to take him away. The remaining seven people are still in custody. Chen Duxiu and the other six people have appealed to the Supreme Court in accordance with the law. On the 2nd, the prosecutor of the Suzhou Higher Court (acting as the plaintiff) also filed a response to the Supreme Court to appeal against Chen and others, asking the court to reject the defendants' appeals. The full response of the prosecutor of the Higher Court is recorded below.

(Response to Chen Peng's Appeal)

The defendants in this case, Chen Duxiu and Peng Shuzhi, organized the Left Opposition faction of the Chinese Communist Party and used words to promote class struggle by inciting workers and poor peasants to revolt, to organize the Soviet Union, to overthrow the National Government of the Kuomintang, and to establish a dictatorship of the proletariat, engaging in treasonous propaganda. The defendants themselves have admitted this without denial, and there is also documentary evidence. The facts of their endangering the Republic of China are extremely clear. The original judgment, based on Article 2, Section 2 and Articles 6 and 74 of the Emergency Law for the Punishment of Acts Endangering the Republic of China, imposes a just sentence and is entirely appropriate.

Reviewing the appeal, it states that countries such as the United Kingdom and the United States do not consider the actions of the Communist Party to be harmful to the state, so why is China different? It should be known that each country has its own political system, and no strong comparisons can be made. The Republic of China has already formulated the Law for the Punishment of Acts Endangering the Republic of China. Since the defendants have violated this law, they should be punished in accordance with the law. The intent of the appeal, which refers to the political systems of other countries, is an attempt to evade responsibility, and its reasoning is therefore not valid.

Furthermore, the appeal states that the National Government is not the state and that overthrowing the government cannot be considered harmful to the Republic of China. The Three Principles of the People are the foundation for the construction of the Republic of China, and the Kuomintang and the National Government are both leading organizations engaged in the construction of the Republic of China. The original judgment has already explained this point in great detail. The Central Opposition faction organized by the defendants aims to overthrow the Three Principles of the People and the National Government of the Kuomintang, which is clearly an act of endangering the Republic of China. The defendants' treasonous propaganda is even more explicit. The intent of the appeal is to deliberately distort the facts, which is difficult to consider reasonable. It is hoped that the original judgment will be upheld and the appeal rejected.

Zhu, Prosecutor of the Jiangsu Higher Court.

(Response to Pu Yifan and Others' Appeal)

Reviewing the appellants' arguments, it is stated that the basis of the judgment is entirely based on speculation and that there is no specific evidence or favorable evidence, and that no investigation has been conducted. On October 15, 1932, Wang Wu (Song Fengchun), Pu Yifan, and Wang Zhaoqun attended a regular weekly meeting of the Communist Party at Xie Shaoshan's home. Xie Shaoshan stated in the Shanghai Public Concession Police Station and the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court that "they were holding their regular weekly meeting when we were arrested." Therefore, the original judgment's recognition of organizing gatherings is not without basis. Wang Wu and Pu Yifan are also candidates for the Central Standing Committee of the Left Opposition faction of the Chinese Communist Party, which has also been clearly stated in separate statements by Xie Shaoshan, Chen Duxiu, and Peng Shuzhi. These statements are all on file and can be reviewed. Guo Jinghao (Peng Daozhi) joined the Communist Party's Opposition faction and engaged in student movements and organizational work. The school registration form (i.e., the Communist Party registration form) seized by the Public Security Bureau contains very detailed records, which are also supported by evidence. The original judgment's basis for conviction is indeed appropriate. The intent of the appeal, which is full of evasive statements, is not reasonable. It is requested that the original judgment be upheld and the appeal rejected.

Zhu, Prosecutor of the Jiangsu Higher Court.

Newspaper Reports on the So-Called Secret Agreement Between the Late Qing Dynasty and Imperial Russia Regarding the Construction of the Chinese Eastern Railway

Since the dispute between the Manchu puppet state and Soviet Russia over the seizure of trains in northern Manchuria in March, Soviet Russia, under pressure from Japan and in order to thoroughly complete the second five-year plan and avoid foreign wars, has disregarded China's sovereignty over the Chinese Eastern Railway and proposed to Japan to sell the railway. Envoys have traveled back and forth for several months, and formal negotiations for the sale finally began in Tokyo on the 27th of last month. Unexpectedly, at this time, the Dongbao newspaper suddenly spread rumors that foreign reporters had discovered a secret agreement between China and Russia when the railway was built. On the same day that the Russo-Japanese-Manchu meeting was held in Tokyo, the Tokyo Asahi Shimbun published a lengthy article by Janice Ward, a Tokyo correspondent for the Chicago Daily News, stating that Russia signed a secret treaty with the Qing government when it built the railway. The purpose was to prevent Japanese attacks and involved France. The original text of Ward's article and the so-called text of the Russo-Chinese secret agreement are translated and await verification by historians. If they are purely fictional, they are enough to expose one aspect of international conspiratorial diplomacy. Based on this, we can further understand the national position of Soviet Russia in selling the railway this time, and the intention of Chicago Daily News reporter Ward in writing the article.

The following is the original text written by Ward.

Historical Recollections: Just Like the Ghost of Long Gone Politicians from Past History, a Secret Sino-Russian Treaty from 1896 Has Been Discovered Today, Causing Trouble for the Current Issue of Selling the North Manchurian Railway.

The outstanding Li Hongzhang and Count Witte have both become people of the underworld. In today's world where Tsarist Russia and the Imperial Qing Dynasty have both disappeared, these recollections of past treaties awaken a kind of evil taint and have become a mockery of current facts. All of this is especially distressing for China and France.

The Sino-Russian-French Alliance

The obvious intention behind this secret treaty is that the railway was built with the purpose of challenging Japan. Therefore, Japan or "Manchukuo," which is a country aided by Japan, would have difficulty demanding the rights and claims of transfer from either France or China. France invested in the railway and was therefore able to obtain a claim to the railway. Similarly, China or "Manchukuo" also has a claim to half of the rights. However, "the loser loses everything" is the natural result of war. Russia was defeated in the Russo-Japanese War, so in terms of the constraints of the treaty, China and France, which formed a secret alliance with Russia, should also be considered to have suffered losses.

The secret treaty was discovered in Moscow. There are legal technical differences. The Russo-Japanese War was resolved by the Treaty of Portsmouth in 1905. If the existence of this secret treaty had been known at that time, the result would likely have been different. Japan could have seized Manchuria as early as 1905, without waiting for September 18, 1931. It would also have acquired the railway earlier than today, as early as 1905.

The Treaty of Portsmouth completed the settlement between Japan and Russia, postponing the determination of the decision between Japan and China and France to a later date. Now, this treaty has been brought out of the ancient chamber, and what is most strange is that the only written copy of the recognized treaty formula is kept in the U.S. State Department in Washington. The original of the Washington Conference Treaty should have been a treasure in the archives of the Soviet and Republic of China governments, but the successive governments in both countries have never published it. The official written copy in the U.S. State Department was acquired after the Washington Conference. At that conference on February 22, 1922, U.S. Secretary of State Hughes recited an abstract of the treaty received from the Chinese representatives, and stated that a full text would be obtained at a later date. The so-called later date means several years after the occasion. It was certainly not included in the report of the conference. The abstract and the full text were finally shelved, so the secret treaty still exists in the archives of the U.S. State Department. The full text is only 400 words, so the Chinese representatives in Washington at the time were able to use the abstract to prevent the Japanese representatives from understanding the true content of the treaty. This is the current speculative observation. The abstract in the telegram at the time and the text of the treaty are identical except for the title, "Sino-Russian Alliance Treaty of 1896." The content is completely different. The abstract in the telegram completely conceals the core of the treaty. For example, the abstract of its first article states, "If Japan attempts any aggression in East Asia against the territories of Russia and China, the two contracting parties will provide appropriate support with all their naval and land forces." However, the first article of the text states, "In East Asia, any aggression by Japan against the territories of Russia, China, or Korea shall be deemed inevitable and shall immediately invoke the application of this treaty. In such circumstances, the two contracting parties shall mutually support each other with all naval and land forces available at the time, and shall agree to provide the greatest possible assistance in supplying food to the forces of each contracting party." The military intention is clear.

As for Article 4, which refers to the Chinese Eastern Railway, the abstract of this article states, "The Chinese government agrees to build a railway line across Heilongjiang Province and Jilin Province in the direction of Unachosk. The Qing Russia Bank (i.e., the Sino-Russian Dao Sheng Bank) is allowed to build and operate the railway line. The contract will be concluded between the Chinese Minister in St. Petersburg and the Qing Russia Bank." This article does not express the military purpose of the railway. However, Article 4 of the text states, "The Chinese government, in order to ensure the means for its troops to easily receive a certain location when the Russian army is invaded, agrees to build a railway line across Heilongjiang Province and Jilin Province in the direction of Unachosk."

Li Hongzhang's Son

The then-Chinese Minister in London was Li Hongzhang's son, who criticized his father's diplomacy. He published his own opinion in the London Daily Review, detailing the beginning and end of the negotiations in 1896 when his father attended the coronation of the Russian Tsar Nicholas. At the time, this article did not attract much attention. It was generally speculated that Russia must have bribed important Chinese officials with large sums of money for the signing of the treaty. The article did not mention this. Only four years later, the former French ambassador to Russia, M. Sernard, published a memoir, which made the treaty document even clearer. Later, at the Versailles Peace Conference in 1919, Chiron also mentioned the treaty in his book on Russia. The official recognition of the treaty was 26 years after the treaty was signed. It expired 11 years later. The publication of the abstract of the telegram at the Washington Conference was later followed by the full text. China also formally recognized it recently. George P. Leesh asked the U.S. State Department to read the written copy of the treaty for Far Eastern affairs. However, the State Department replied that the full text in the MacMurray Treaties was no different from the "unofficial written copy of the French text." Only the U.S. State Department, which holds the French text, knows the truth.

The Full Text of the So-Called Secret Qing-Russian Treaty at the Time of the Construction of the Chinese Eastern Railway

The next day after the above article was published (June 28), the Asahi Shimbun published the full text of the secret treaty, stating that the construction cost of the Chinese Eastern Railway was actually paid by France. At the time, China and Russia concluded a secret treaty, which was unknown to outsiders for 23 years. The text of the secret treaty is now revealed as follows:

Article 1: In East Asia, any aggression by Japan against the territories of Russia, China, or Korea shall be deemed inevitable and shall immediately invoke the application of this treaty. In such circumstances, the two contracting parties shall mutually support each other with all naval and land forces available at the time, and shall agree to provide the greatest possible assistance in supplying food to the forces of each contracting party.

Article 2: After the two contracting parties begin joint activities, neither contracting party may conclude a peace treaty with the enemy without the consent of the other party.

Article 3: In the event of war, all ports of Qing China shall, if necessary, be used by Russian warships, and the Qing government authorities shall provide all necessary assistance.

Article 4: The Chinese government, fearing that Russian troops would be vulnerable to invasion and in order to ensure the means for its troops to easily reach a certain location, agrees to build a railway line across Heilongjiang Province and Jilin Province in the direction of Unachosk. The connection of the railway with the Russian railway shall not be used as a pretext to infringe upon the territory of Qing China and the sovereignty of the Qing Emperor. The terms for concluding a contract for the construction and operation of the railway by the Qing Russia Bank shall be formally discussed between the Qing Minister in St. Petersburg and the Qing Russia Bank.

Article 5: In the event of war, Russia may freely use the railway described in Article 4 for the transportation of troops and the supply of food, as described in Article 1. In peacetime, Russia shall retain the same rights for the transportation of troops and goods, but shall not be allowed to stop except when necessary for transportation.

Article 6: The terms of Article 4 of this treaty shall come into effect when the Qing Emperor approves it. This treaty shall be valid for fifteen years from that time. Six months before the expiration of the term, the two contracting parties may consider extending its duration.

Songjiang Asks the Ministry of Finance to Stop the New Liquor Tax

The Sijing Township Chamber of Commerce believes that the newly established liquor tax is harassing merchants and petitions the Ministry of Finance to stop it. The text of the petition is recorded below.

Petition: Regarding the New Liquor Tax Regulations Harassing Merchants, We Urgently Request a Stop.

According to a letter from the Jiangzao Industry Association of our township, domestic liquors have been subject to the public sales tax. Recently, the Tax Administration has drastically changed the original public sales tax, implementing a fixed-amount tax on domestic liquors, which will be implemented on July 1. The tax rate regulations are complex and severe, and the penalties are heavy. Once implemented, not only will merchants be unable to bear the burden, but even minor oversights in the procedures will lead to legal trouble. This is tantamount to destroying domestic liquors, while imported foreign liquors can be sold unhindered. The future of the industry is unimaginable. We urge your association to forward this petition to stop this tax in order to leave a ray of hope for domestic goods and to prevent endless suffering for the industry.

We have investigated and found that commerce is failing at an alarming rate. Now, the liquor merchants are burdened with a harassing fixed-amount tax, which is unbearable. Therefore, we have prepared this petition and sincerely request the Minister to quickly stop this tax.

Authorities Discuss Revising Train Schedules

For the convenience of passengers, the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways have revised their train schedules, reducing the travel time of the Beijing-Shanghai express train to within seven hours. The travel time of other passenger trains has also been reduced accordingly. In addition, the operating intervals of local trains have been extended, and more stations have been added. Since the implementation on June 1st, passengers have found it convenient. Recently, due to environmental needs, further revisions have been made. A reporter from the Central News Agency specially visited Mr. Si, the person in charge, yesterday to inquire about the reasons for these revisions. Mr. Si provided a detailed explanation, which is summarized below.

Early Departure of Upbound Connecting Train

The upbound Domestic Joint Transportation Special Train No. 302, which was previously scheduled to depart from the North Station at 1 AM, has been rescheduled to depart at 9:50 PM. Since the preparation for the Capital Ferry began, the Railway Department ordered the planning of a direct train between Ping and Shanghai. Representatives from the Beijing-Ning, Tianjin-Pukou, and Beijing-Shanghai Railways held a meeting in Beijing, where the three railways agreed that the upbound train would depart from Pukou every morning. The Tianjin-Pukou Railway planned to implement the newly revised schedule for the connecting train starting on July 1st. At that time, this railway scheduled the train to depart from Shanghai at 1 AM every day in order to ensure that passengers would not have to wait too long after arriving at Beijing Station. Therefore, passengers traveling between Ping and Shanghai on the connecting train would continue to be transported by the existing Train No. 301 (the original Train No. 4) for the downbound journey, while the upbound journey would be temporarily transported by the existing Train No. 4 express train. However, it was recently learned that the Tianjin-Pukou Railway's newly revised schedule could not be implemented as scheduled due to various reasons. In order to facilitate passengers and avoid overcrowding on the original night express train, this railway decided to advance the departure time of the connecting train to 9:50 PM from the North Station, arriving in Nanjing at 6:10 AM the next morning, before the connecting train truly reaches the Tianjin-Pukou Railway. This new schedule has been implemented since June 22nd.

Later Arrival of Wuxi-Shanghai Local Train

The first Wuxi-Shanghai local train still departs from Wuxi Station at 6 AM and has not been changed. However, after the train arrives at Suzhou Station, it must wait 13 minutes to meet Train No. 14, wait 8 minutes at Weiting Station to meet Train No. 12, wait 22 minutes at Zhengyi Station to meet Train No. 8, wait 28 minutes at Kunshan Station to meet Train No. 16, and wait 9 minutes at Huangdu Station to meet Train No. 4. In total, the waiting time at the stations, in addition to the scheduled stops, takes nearly an hour. Since Trains No. 4, 8, and 12 are all direct trains to Shanghai and Beijing, they should be given priority. Even Trains No. 14 and 16, which are also local trains, are affected by the issue of meeting other trains, making it inevitable to delay the early Wuxi-Shanghai local train. As a result, the arrival time of the local train in Shanghai is 35 minutes later than before. This is due to the difficulties of meeting trains along the single-track line, making it practically unavoidable. This delay can be reduced after the implementation of future route improvement plans.

Reasons for Delayed Departure of Downbound Connecting Train

The newly added Train No. 301, a downbound domestic connecting express train, is the original Beijing-Shanghai downbound Train No. 4 special express train. After the ferry between Beijing and Pukou begins, the departure time from Beijing must be delayed in order to connect with the Tianjin-Pukou Railway's train schedule. In addition, Train No. 9, a medium-speed train between Beijing and Shanghai, is designed to facilitate passengers traveling from Nanjing to Shanghai at noon, and its departure time cannot be too early. Therefore, the arrival time in Shanghai cannot be advanced.

Cancellation of Noon Express After Adding Connecting Train

After adding upbound and downbound domestic connecting express trains on the Beijing-Shanghai Line, the downbound train is operated by the original Beijing-Shanghai Train No. 4 express train. The upbound train, because it must arrive at Beijing Station every morning to connect with the Tianjin-Pukou Railway, an additional upbound train (No. 302) must be added every night. However, due to a shortage of locomotives, the original Shanghai-Beijing noon express train was canceled, and the saved locomotive power was used for the connecting train. After the cancellation of the Shanghai-Beijing noon express train, passengers traveling from Shanghai to stations within the Zhenjiang section can take the newly revised Shanghai-Zhenjiang local train (formerly the Shanghai-Changzhou local train, now extended to Zhenjiang). Passengers traveling from Shanghai to Beijing can take the upbound Train No. 2 Zha Jing express train, which departs from the North Station at 3:10 PM. The travel time has been shortened, and the arrival time in Beijing is similar to the original noon express train, which is still convenient for passengers.

Earlier Departure of Beijing-Xuzhou Local Train

The Beijing-Xuzhou local train was originally scheduled to depart at 5 PM, but it has been advanced to 2 PM. There are three reasons for the earlier departure: 1. After the original Train No. 4 special express train was changed to Train No. 301 domestic connecting train, the departure time was delayed to 5:25 PM. If the local train still departs from Beijing around 5 PM, the two trains would be too close together, and the local train would likely be overtaken by Train No. 301 along the way. 2. After the noon express train departs from Beijing Station at 12:40 PM, downbound passengers must wait until 5:25 PM for the next train, which is too long and inconvenient. Therefore, the local train was advanced to the scheduled time to facilitate passengers. 3. The arrival time of the local train in Xuzhou was too late, which was also inconvenient for passengers. Therefore, the departure time from Beijing was advanced to allow passengers traveling to Xuzhou to arrive earlier.

Beijing-Zhenjiang Local Train to Be Launched Soon

The Railway Bureau revised the schedule to facilitate passengers traveling between Nanjing, the capital, and Zhenjiang, the provincial capital, by adding a local train between Beijing and Zhenjiang in both directions. However, the Zhenjiang Station's facilities, such as the locomotive turntable and passenger car depot, have not yet been completed, so it has not been possible to start operations. The Railway Bureau is making every effort to expedite its completion to facilitate passengers.

Shanghai-Changzhou Local Train Extended to Zhenjiang

To facilitate passengers traveling between Shanghai and Zhenjiang, the Railway Bureau extended the original Shanghai-Changzhou local train to Zhenjiang, renaming it the Shanghai-Zhenjiang Train No. 22. At the same time, the original Changzhou-Shanghai local train was renamed the Zhenjiang-Shanghai Train No. 21 and started operating from Zhenjiang. Starting on June 22nd, the upbound Train No. 22 will make additional stops at Xinzha Zhen, Lucheng, Lingkou, and the South Gate of Zhenjiang. The downbound Train No. 21 will make an additional stop at Luoshe Station. Tickets will be sold to and from these stations to facilitate passengers.

Criminal Wu Bangyin Dies of Injuries Sustained While Resisting Arrest

On the afternoon of December 19th of last year, at 7 PM, Chinese Constables No. 3120 and 3137 of the Gordon Road Police Station encountered four pedestrians on Singapore Road who were acting suspiciously. The constables immediately ordered them to stop for questioning. Unexpectedly, one of them drew a pistol, intending to open fire on the constables. However, the gun was damaged, so although the trigger was pulled, no bullets were fired. The constables, seeing the situation as extremely dangerous, also drew their pistols and fired several shots at him, hitting him in the legs and other areas. After being wounded, the man fell to the ground and was arrested. The other three took the opportunity to escape. The constables transported the injured man to the Gongbu Hospital for treatment and reported the incident to the police station. After further investigation, it was learned that the man was named Wu Bangyin, 30 years old. It was suspected that he and the other fugitives intended to rob a cigarette paper store on Connaught Road that day, but they were caught on the way. Wu died of his injuries the day before yesterday. His body was taken to the Xielun Road morgue. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Court dispatched Prosecutor Guo Wei to the morgue to examine the body. After questioning Constables No. 3120 and 3137, and presenting the pistol for inspection, Mr. Guo ruled that the deceased, Wu Bangyin, died from gunshot wounds sustained while resisting arrest. The body was handed over to the Pushan Cemetery for burial. The deceased was found to be carrying a pistol, seven bullets, and one spent shell, which were temporarily handed over to the police station's gun room for safekeeping.

Two Corpses (Headless Girl)

The South Wharf Rescue Bureau's patrol boat recovered a child's body in the Huangpu River the day before yesterday. The child was about six or seven years old and was wearing a calico dress. The child was female, but her head was missing, apparently having been cut off. It is unknown whose child has suffered this tragic fate. The incident was immediately reported to the court, which dispatched a prosecutor to examine the body. The body was ordered to be taken to the morgue to await identification by family members. After questioning, further investigation will be conducted.

(Nie A'mei Dies)

Nie A'mei, a 40-year-old boat dweller from Ningbo, was working on barge No. 222. The day before yesterday, while traveling to the Taikoo Wharf, Nie lost his footing while punting the boat and fell into the river, drowning instantly. The boat owner reported the incident to the water police station, which contacted the Rescue Bureau. Yesterday, the body was recovered and taken to the South Wharf riverside. The incident was reported to the local court, and the prosecutor arrived to examine the body, confirming that the cause of death was drowning. The body was ordered to be taken to the morgue to await instructions.

Publishing Industry Author Bookstore Latest News

In recent years, the number of Chinese-language works by Chinese authors has been increasing. However, due to a lack of promotion methods, sales have been sluggish. As a result, authors must still rely on bookstores for consignment sales. However, each bookstore has its own books to publish and distribute, so they cannot focus on promoting other authors' works. Last autumn, a new force emerged: the Author Bookstore, which specializes in consignment sales of works by individuals and academic organizations. This type of independent consignment business has thin profits, which has long been recognized by both the writing and reading communities. Given the high cost of rent and other expenses in Shanghai, it is admirable that the bookstore's manager, Mr. Huang Buxiang, pays authors promptly for their actual sales and never defaults. The bookstore also adheres to the principle of small profits and quick turnover for readers and does not charge high prices. With such determination and spirit, authors across the country are happy to cooperate and entrust the bookstore to distribute their works. The bookstore has recently become the center for the distribution of individual works. It is also offering discount coupons for purchasing books, which can be obtained by mail or in person.

Free Talk The Formation of Experts - Lin Weiyin

If you have perseverance, that is, if you are willing to say the same thing over and over again, it is not difficult for you to become an expert. For example, if you want to become a wine-tasting expert, then you can write an article today saying what are the uses of drinking wine, and write an article tomorrow saying how people who do not drink wine are not poetic or heroic, or say anything, as long as you say it. You can also find examples from Chinese and foreign history, no, just from literary history (this can also incidentally prove that you are a literary figure, because you are so familiar with anecdotes in literary history, it is impossible for people not to believe that you are a literary figure) to say that poet so-and-so could drink three dou in one breath, and novelist so-and-so could drink continuously for seven days without stopping. Or you can far-fetchedly say that whoever drinks more wine has a son who is a genius; or whoever cannot write good articles is because they do not drink wine. Or you can even make up a story saying how those who cannot get wine to drink substitute it with tea with some salt, which can further prove that wine is always indispensable in any environment. And you have to say it as if it were true, as if people don't drink wine or don't know how to drink wine. If they do, it is because of your articles. Then your wine-tasting expert is undoubtedly formed, and later when someone mentions wine, they must mention you and your articles about wine. At the same time, there is another benefit; if your wife does not allow you to drink, you can speak with confidence; or if you yourself think that drinking wine is harmful to your health, but you are unwilling not to drink it, you can also slightly justify yourself with this. Also, you should not think that because you are not good at drinking, you cannot proclaim all of the above; on the contrary, those who are not good at it will proclaim it with great relish. For example, if you say how good a certain dish is, perhaps it is precisely because you do not often eat that dish. Someone who praises opium is someone who is not addicted, at most it only proves that he has smoked opium, and someone who is addicted will not praise it everywhere. So don't worry, the wine-tasting expert is yours.

On "Scholars Without Morals" - Gu Chunfan

Although I myself am also a member of the so-called "scholarly" "forest," I have recently expressed some agreement with the saying "scholars without morals," and I do not completely regard the lamentations of "people's hearts are not as good as they used to be" and "the world is going downhill" as the extreme words of "moralistic gentlemen." Indeed, today's "human hearts" are too terribly treacherous, especially the so-called "scholars," who can come up with and do all kinds of despicable behaviors such as scheming and slandering, spreading rumors and defaming, publicly informing, and selling friends for glory or selling themselves for refuge, the list is endless. And on the other hand, self-promotion, shamelessly claiming to be a "genius" or "writer," and stealing the leftovers of others' saliva, while still feeling pleased with themselves, are also all kinds of strange phenomena of "nothing ugly is missing, and all evils are reached." Facing these heartbreaking facts, can we still deny the considerable truth of the saying "scholars without morals"? (Of course, I am not saying that all scholars are without morals.) Can we not feel the lamentations of "the way of the world and people's hearts"? Of course, my feelings are not without reason. To give a real example, there was someone named Zeng, who insisted on using nonsense like "who cares" and "playing mahjong" to practice his so-called "liberation of lyrics," and was rebuked as a "frivolous youth" and a "lustful eager of sex." Zeng babbled on and on, defending himself endlessly. Now, new facts have again proved that Zeng is not only a frivolous youth, but also a venomous and hateful snake. He can use Cui Wanqiu's name to brag about himself (see Cui's advertisement in this newspaper in February), and even forcibly assign a Japanese typist and a middle school teacher to be "female poets" and "university professors," praising himself meticulously; he can use the most despicable means to submit articles to tabloids, pointing out his friends as XXX and publishing their addresses, publicly selling his friends (see the 5th issue of Sino-Foreign Books and Newspapers News). Such boldness, such venom, such boredom, really makes me unable to believe that this is something that a "person" with a sense of shame and personality, especially a "scholar," can do. However, Zeng really can come up with it and really can do it. I think anyone cannot but admire Zeng's fearless spirit. I heard that Zeng is not very old and has not had the opportunity to study. I think if Zeng could put that kind of energy in bragging and flattering and that kind of venomous and ingenious mind into seeking real knowledge, wouldn't he gain more? However, Zeng insists on spending his days bragging and flattering, and spending his days creating rumors and slandering. This, on the one hand, makes Zeng's terribleness even more apparent, and on the other hand, it also shows the pity of youth being misled. However, to go back to the main point, even those who have received higher education may not necessarily be able to restrain themselves. For example, Zhang XX, who is famous for writing stories of triangular love and has made a fortune, often boasts of being from a certain school in Japan. However, he has also recently been yelling and cursing in some tabloids, with the face of a "rejected woman" full of hatred. He will scheme and slander, create rumors and provoke, and he will forcibly assign people to be like Bukharin or Lenin, simply wanting to put you to death. His despicable personality and vicious means can be said to be unprecedented. In this light, what is the use of higher education? There is also an article in a newly published boring publication signed "Bai Yuxia," entitled "Sitting in Uchiyama Bookstore," which openly says that someone often goes to Uchiyama Bookstore and has asked Uchiyama Bookstore to save their life and provide insurance. I think this kind of public informing is probably a trick played by second-rate people using pseudonyms. However, no matter how they spread rumors and slander, and no matter how they scheme and frame, discerning people will know at a glance that harming others will not work, but will only expose their own baseness and lack of personality. But, I think that "scholars" "with morals" really should not continue to ignore these ugly types as they do now, but should rise up and drive them out of the literary world. They should do a cleaning

Yuan Chun, Wan Xing, Yuan Heng, Zhao Feng, Chang Yong Feng, and others bought strongly, raising the price to $8.00. Chartered Bank sold September US dollars at 2.5, plus advance knowledge of a US dollar increase of $1.25 and a UK increase of 1.25, so it retreated within $5.00. Shun Li, Da Xing, and Yong also came to sell September US dollars at 2.5 and October US dollars at 4.375, both proving difficult to settle and rising to $7.50. Wayfoong sold September US dollars at 1.875. The noon close was $856.40. Commodities closed at $6.50.

Later, Hong Li and Shun Li jointly sold, and Wayfoong released September US dollars at 2.5, and Bank of China offered October at 4.375, causing the price to fall from $6.50 to within $5.00. Although banks took in small amounts of October half-dollars, peers wanted to sell but couldn't. Yuan Sheng, Yong Qian, Chang Xiang, and Rui Kang sold at $3.00, and short-sellers covered, pushing it up by more than one dollar. But Bombay reported a rise of one anna, with unfavorable rumors, causing selling to surge. Zhi Feng Yong, Tian Feng Yong, Shun Li, Da De Cheng, Yuan Mao, Chang Sheng Yong, sold down to $0.05. Heng Yu bought slightly, pushing it back up to over $2.00, but large firms seemed to be forceful in supplying. Chartered Bank wanted 6.875 for October US dollars, but it was difficult. The Tendency is Toward Recession; The Dangerous Period Has Passed 57

(Nanjing) The Yangtze River Channel Improvement Committee issued the following report on water levels in various locations along the river on the 4th: (1) Upper reaches: Chongqing 32.0 feet, 4.0 feet higher than the 3rd; Wanxian 38.1 feet, 2.6 feet higher than the 3rd; Yichang 21.8 feet, 0.4 feet lower than the 3rd; Shashi 18.7 feet, 0.7 feet lower than the 3rd. (2) Middle reaches: Yuezhou 43.7 feet, 0.8 feet lower than the 3rd; Hankou 45.7 feet, 0.3 feet lower than the 3rd; Jiujiang 43.7 feet, 0.2 feet lower than the 3rd; Anqing, details unknown.
