According to the above table, only Chongqing and Wanxian in the upper reaches show a slight increase, and Nanjing and Zhenjiang in the lower reaches show a slight upward trend. The rest are all trending downward, and it is expected that the dangerous period of river flooding has already passed. (Central News Agency dispatch, 4th)

Hankou River Water Continues to Recede 58

(Hankou) The river water receded two and a half inches on the 4th, the water mark is 45 feet 7 and a half inches. Yichang is stable. The Hubei provincial flood prevention fund is 200,000 yuan. The Jianghan Engineering Bureau is now considering the length of the embankment sections, the degree of danger, and traffic conditions to properly allocate the funds. (Special dispatch, 4th)

(Hankou) Eleven watchtowers on the Wuchang Baoshan embankment were washed away by the water, resulting in multiple deaths by drowning. On the 4th, the bodies of four men and women were recovered. (Special dispatch, 4th)

Japanese Salvaging Sunken Warship 59

(Hankou) After the Japanese "Nitami" warship sank, the "Atsumi" and "Seto" warships are currently carrying out salvage operations under the command of engineer Saito. A large number of artillery shells and bullets, worth more than 400,000, have been recovered. Important machinery still remains. A telegram has been sent to Shanghai to send additional engineers to assist with the salvage. It is planned to abandon the ship's hull in the river. Mr. Mibe, a Japanese interpreter in Hankou, unfortunately perished in this incident. (Special dispatch, 4th)

(Nanchang) An announcement was made stating that Zhu and Mao's main force, which had advanced to Neihuang, retreated desperately to the south after our army arrived in force and engaged in fierce fighting. We have blockaded and are monitoring the bandits, and will annihilate them once the Guangdong and Fujian armies arrive at the designated location. (Special dispatch, 4th)

National Government Abolishes the Outline for Military Law Joint Trial Organizations 63

(Nanjing) Based on a resolution of the Central Political Council, the National Government ordered the Executive and Judicial Yuan to abolish the "Outline for Military Law Joint Trial Organizations" and the "Provisional Military Law Trial Regulations of Various Provinces." (Special dispatch, 4th)

Ministry of Interior Establishes Land Law and Regulations Committee 64

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Interior has established a Land Law and Regulations Committee with 19 members. The Director and section chiefs of the Land Department will be ex-officio members. In addition, the General Staff Headquarters will recommend three personnel above the recommended rank, and the Ministries of Justice, Industry, Finance, Foreign Affairs, and Military Affairs will each recommend one person of the selected rank and one person with rich knowledge and experience in land. A chairman will be appointed, concurrently held by the Director of the Land Department. A regular meeting will be held once a month to revise various land laws and regulations. (Special dispatch, 4th)

Sun Ke and Others Return to Nanjing from Shanghai 68

(Nanjing) Sun Ke and Ma Chaojun returned to Nanjing from Shanghai by train on the night of the 4th. (Central News Agency dispatch, 4th)

Progress in the Business of the China Merchants Bureau 69

(Nanjing) Liu Hongsheng, General Manager of the China Merchants Bureau, reported to the Ministry of Communications on the 3rd that since the Bureau became state-owned, from December of last year to May of this year, the total revenue was more than 2,364,500 yuan, an increase of more than 400,000 yuan compared to the same period in the previous four years. It is hoped that revenue and expenditure can be offset this year, and the business is progressing and the future is promising. (Central News Agency dispatch, 4th)

Wang Orders All Agencies Not to Shorten Office Hours 70

(Nanjing) Various ministries and commissions of the Executive Yuan have shortened office hours due to the hot weather, and afternoon breaks have already been implemented in the Ministries of Foreign Affairs, Industry, and Railways, as well as the Judicial Administration Department. The Ministries of Transportation and Education are still working full days, but Premier Wang does not quite agree. On the 4th, he issued a special order to all subordinate agencies not to change to half-day office hours during the summer season. (Central News Agency dispatch, 4th)

Long-Term Lectures by the Statistics Federation 71

(Nanjing) The Central Agencies Statistics Federation, in view of the rapid development of statistical science, should exchange ideas and conduct research in order to make progress. It is now planned to have a systematic long-term lecture series, divided into theoretical and experimental aspects. Experts will be hired to be in charge, and all statistical personnel from various agencies will attend the lectures. The duration will be one year, once a month for two hours each time. This month's session will begin with Wu Dajun, Director of the Accounting Department's Statistics Bureau, as chairman. (Central News Agency dispatch, 4th)

Heads of Provincial Reformatories Will Be Appointed 72

(Nanjing) The heads of the provincial reformatories were originally appointed by the Ministry of Judicial Administration. After a resolution by the Central Political Conference, the heads of the reformatories must be nominated by the central government and appointed by the government. Currently, except for Liao Weifan, head of the Capital Reformatory, who has already been appointed, the heads of the remaining provincial reformatories have also been internally decided and will be submitted for a simplified appointment soon. (Central News Agency dispatch, 4th)
